# 吃饱了吗点餐平台

Tianjin University Software Engineering Project

Base URLs:

- <a href="http://localhost:8080/elm">开发环境: <http://localhost:8080/elm></a>

# Authentication

- HTTP Authentication, scheme: bearer
- HTTP Authentication, scheme: bearer

# 管理店铺

<a id="opIdgetBusiness"></a>

## GET getBusiness

GET /api/businesses/{id}

### 请求参数

| 名称 | 位置   | 类型             | 必选 | 说明   |
| -- | ---- | -------------- | -- | ---- |
| id | path | integer(int64) | 是  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"businessName":"string","businessOwner":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"businessAddress":"string","businessExplain":"string","businessImg":"string","orderTypeId":0,"startPrice":0,"deliveryPrice":0,"remarks":"string"},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                            |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultBusiness](#schemahttpresultbusiness) |

<a id="opIdupdateBusiness"></a>

## PUT updateBusiness

PUT /api/businesses/{id}

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "businessName": "string",
  "businessOwner": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  },
  "businessAddress": "string",
  "businessExplain": "string",
  "businessImg": "string",
  "orderTypeId": 0,
  "startPrice": 0,
  "deliveryPrice": 0,
  "remarks": "string"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                          | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | --------------------------- | -- | ---- |
| id   | path | integer(int64)              | 是  | none |
| body | body | [Business](#schemabusiness) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"businessName":"string","businessOwner":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"businessAddress":"string","businessExplain":"string","businessImg":"string","orderTypeId":0,"startPrice":0,"deliveryPrice":0,"remarks":"string"},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                            |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultBusiness](#schemahttpresultbusiness) |

<a id="opIddeleteBusiness"></a>

## DELETE deleteBusiness

DELETE /api/businesses/{id}

### 请求参数

| 名称 | 位置   | 类型             | 必选 | 说明   |
| -- | ---- | -------------- | -- | ---- |
| id | path | integer(int64) | 是  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":"string","message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称        | 类型          | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| --------- | ----------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| » success | boolean     | false | none | <br /> | none |
| » code    | string      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| » data    | string      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| » message | string¦null | false | none | <br /> | none |

<a id="opIdpatchBusiness"></a>

## PATCH patchBusiness

PATCH /api/businesses/{id}

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "businessName": "string",
  "businessOwner": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  },
  "businessAddress": "string",
  "businessExplain": "string",
  "businessImg": "string",
  "orderTypeId": 0,
  "startPrice": 0,
  "deliveryPrice": 0,
  "remarks": "string"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                          | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | --------------------------- | -- | ---- |
| id   | path | integer(int64)              | 是  | none |
| body | body | [Business](#schemabusiness) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"businessName":"string","businessOwner":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"businessAddress":"string","businessExplain":"string","businessImg":"string","orderTypeId":0,"startPrice":0,"deliveryPrice":0,"remarks":"string"},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                            |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultBusiness](#schemahttpresultbusiness) |

## POST addBusiness

POST /api/businesses

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "businessName": "string",
  "businessOwner": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  },
  "businessAddress": "string",
  "businessExplain": "string",
  "businessImg": "string",
  "orderTypeId": 0,
  "startPrice": 0,
  "deliveryPrice": 0,
  "remarks": "string"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                          | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | --------------------------- | -- | ---- |
| body | body | [Business](#schemabusiness) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"businessName":"string","businessOwner":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"businessAddress":"string","businessExplain":"string","businessImg":"string","orderTypeId":0,"startPrice":0,"deliveryPrice":0,"remarks":"string"},"message":"string"}
```

<a id="opIdgetCurrentUserBusinesses"></a>

## GET 获取当前用户的店铺

GET /api/businesses/my

获取当前登录用户所拥有的所有店铺列表

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":[{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"businessName":"string","businessOwner":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":null}]},"businessAddress":"string","businessExplain":"string","businessImg":"string","orderTypeId":0,"startPrice":0,"deliveryPrice":0,"remarks":"string"}],"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                                    |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ------------------------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultListBusiness](#schemahttpresultlistbusiness) |

# 管理用户

<a id="opIdcreateUser"></a>

## POST 新增用户（包括密码）

POST /api/users

创建一个新的用户（仅登录帐号）

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "username": "string",
  "password": "string",
  "rememberMe": true
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                          | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | --------------------------- | -- | ---- |
| body | body | [LoginDto](#schemalogindto) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                    |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | --------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultUser](#schemahttpresultuser) |

<a id="opIdgetAllUsers"></a>

## GET 获取所有用户

GET /api/users

获取所有用户的列表，主要用于管理界面

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":[{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]}],"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                            |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultListUser](#schemahttpresultlistuser) |

<a id="opIdaddPerson"></a>

## POST 新增用户（自然人）

POST /api/persons

创建一个新的用户（自然人）
必需参数：username，默认密码password，默认权限User，同时会创建一个User

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "username": "string",
  "authorities": [
    {
      "name": "string"
    }
  ],
  "firstName": "string",
  "lastName": "string",
  "email": "string",
  "phone": "string",
  "gender": "string",
  "photo": "string"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                      | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | ----------------------- | -- | ---- |
| body | body | [Person](#schemaperson) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}],"firstName":"string","lastName":"string","email":"string","phone":"string","gender":"string","photo":"string"},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                        |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ------------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultPerson](#schemahttpresultperson) |

<a id="opIdupdateUserPassword"></a>

## POST 修改密码

POST /api/password

已登录的用户只可以修改自己的密码，Admin可以修改任何人的密码

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "username": "string",
  "password": "string",
  "rememberMe": true
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                          | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | --------------------------- | -- | ---- |
| body | body | [LoginDto](#schemalogindto) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":"string","message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称        | 类型          | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| --------- | ----------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| » success | boolean     | false | none | <br /> | none |
| » code    | string      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| » data    | string      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| » message | string¦null | false | none | <br /> | none |

<a id="opIdgetUserById"></a>

## GET 根据ID获取用户

GET /api/users/{id}

查询单个用户的详细信息

### 请求参数

| 名称 | 位置   | 类型             | 必选 | 说明   |
| -- | ---- | -------------- | -- | ---- |
| id | path | integer(int64) | 是  | 用户ID |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                    |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | --------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultUser](#schemahttpresultuser) |

<a id="opIdupdateUser"></a>

## PUT 更新用户信息

PUT /api/users/{id}

更新指定ID用户的详细信息

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "username": "string",
  "authorities": [
    {
      "name": "string"
    }
  ],
  "firstName": "string",
  "lastName": "string",
  "email": "string",
  "phone": "string",
  "gender": "string",
  "photo": "string"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置   | 类型                      | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---- | ---- | ----------------------- | -- | ---- |
| id   | path | integer(int64)          | 是  | 用户ID |
| body | body | [Person](#schemaperson) | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```
{"success":true,"code":"string","data":{"id":0,"createTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","updateTime":"2019-08-24T14:15:22Z","creator":0,"updater":0,"deleted":true,"username":"string","authorities":[{"name":"string"}]},"message":"string"}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明 | 数据模型                                    |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | -- | --------------------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | OK | [HttpResultUser](#schemahttpresultuser) |

# 管理订单

## GET getMyOrders(Customer)

GET /api/orders/user/my

根据token的用户信息，获取该消费者的所有订单

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": [
    {
      "id": 0,
      "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "creator": 0,
      "updater": 0,
      "deleted": true,
      "customer": {
        "id": 0,
        "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "creator": 0,
        "updater": 0,
        "deleted": true,
        "username": "string",
        "authorities": [
          {
            "name": null
          }
        ]
      },
      "business": {
        "id": 0,
        "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "creator": 0,
        "updater": 0,
        "deleted": true,
        "businessName": "string",
        "businessOwner": {
          "id": 0,
          "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
          "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
          "creator": 0,
          "updater": 0,
          "deleted": true,
          "username": "string",
          "authorities": [
            null
          ]
        },
        "businessAddress": "string",
        "businessExplain": "string",
        "businessImg": "string",
        "orderTypeId": 0,
        "startPrice": 0,
        "deliveryPrice": 0,
        "remarks": "string"
      },
      "orderDate": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "orderTotal": 0,
      "deliveryAddress": {
        "id": 0,
        "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "creator": 0,
        "updater": 0,
        "deleted": true,
        "contactName": "string",
        "contactSex": 0,
        "contactTel": "string",
        "address": "string",
        "customer": {
          "id": 0,
          "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
          "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
          "creator": 0,
          "updater": 0,
          "deleted": true,
          "username": "string",
          "authorities": [
            null
          ]
        }
      },
      "orderState": 0
    }
  ],
  "message": "string"
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

## GET getOrdersByBusinessId

## GET listOrdersByUserId

### 请求参数

| 名称     | 位置    | 类型             | 必选 | 说明   |
| ------ | ----- | -------------- | -- | ---- |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response


# 管理认证

## POST refresh

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "refresh_token": "string"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称               | 位置   | 类型     | 必选 | 说明   |
| ---------------- | ---- | ------ | -- | ---- |
| body             | body | object | 否  | none |
| » refresh\_token | body | string | 是  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "id_token": "string"
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型                        |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | --------------------------- |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | [JWTToken](#schemajwttoken) |

```json
    "deleted": true,
```
```json
    "businessName": "string",
    "businessOwner": {
      "id": 0,
```

| » deleted            | body | boolean                          | 否  | none |

| »» id                | body | integer(int64)                   | 是  | none |
| »» createTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» updateTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |

| »»» createTime       | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »»» updateTime       | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |

| »» deliveryPrice     | body | number                           | 否  | none |
| »» remarks           | body | string                           | 否  | none |
| » handler            | body | [User](#schemauser)              | 否  | none |
| »» id                | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» createTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» updateTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» creator           | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» updater           | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |

```json
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": {
    "id": 0,

    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "business": {
      "id": 0,
      "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",

      "deleted": true,
      "businessName": "string",
      "businessOwner": {
        "id": 0,

        "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
        "creator": 0,
        "updater": 0,
```

# 管理商家申请

## POST 提交商家申请

POST /api/applications/merchant

用户申请商家

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "applicant": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  },
  "applicationExplain": "string",
  "applicationState": 0,
  "handler": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称                   | 位置   | 类型                               | 必选 | 说明   |
| -------------------- | ---- | -------------------------------- | -- | ---- |
| body                 | body | object                           | 否  | none |
| » id                 | body | integer(int64)                   | 是  | none |
| » createTime         | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| » updateTime         | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| » creator            | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| » updater            | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| » deleted            | body | boolean                          | 否  | none |
| » applicant          | body | [User](#schemauser)              | 是  | none |
| »» id                | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» createTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» updateTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» creator           | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» updater           | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» deleted           | body | boolean                          | 否  | none |
| »» username          | body | string                           | 是  | none |
| »» authorities       | body | \[[Authority](#schemaauthority)] | 否  | none |
| »»» name             | body | string                           | 是  | none |
| » applicationExplain | body | string                           | 否  | none |
| » applicationState   | body | integer(int32)                   | 否  | none |
| » handler            | body | [User](#schemauser)              | 否  | none |
| »» id                | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» createTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» updateTime        | body | string(date-time)                | 否  | none |
| »» creator           | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» updater           | body | integer(int64)                   | 否  | none |
| »» deleted           | body | boolean                          | 否  | none |
| »» username          | body | string                           | 是  | none |
| »» authorities       | body | \[[Authority](#schemaauthority)] | 否  | none |

> 返回示例

## GET 获取订单评价

GET /api/reviews/order/{orderId}

获取指定订单评价

> Body 请求参数

```json
null
```

### 请求参数

| 名称      | 位置   | 类型             | 必选 | 说明   |
| ------- | ---- | -------------- | -- | ---- |

| body    | body | null           | 否  | none |

## PATCH 修改评价

PATCH /api/reviews/{reviewId}

用户修改评价（仅能修改stars, content和anonymous）

# 管理钱包

## GET getWalletById

GET /api/wallet/{id}

通过walletId查询钱包

### 请求参数

| 名称 | 位置   | 类型             | 必选 | 说明   |
| -- | ---- | -------------- | -- | ---- |
| id | path | integer(int64) | 是  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": {
    "id": 0,
    "owner": 0,
    "balance": 0,
    "voucher": 0
  },
  "message": "string"
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称         | 类型                      | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| ---------- | ----------------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| » success  | boolean                 | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| » code     | string                  | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| » data     | [Wallet](#schemawallet) | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| »» id      | integer(int64)          | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| »» owner   | integer(int64)          | false | none | <br /> | none |
| »» balance | integer(int64)          | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| »» voucher | integer(int64)          | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| » message  | string¦null             | false | none | <br /> | none |

```json
    "amount": 0,

      }
```

# 管理公共优惠券

## GET 获取所有公共优惠券

GET /api/publicVoucher/list

仅管理员可用，获取所有公共优惠券信息

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": [
    {
      "id": 0,
      "threshold": 0,
      "value": 0,
      "claimable": true,
      "validDays": 0
    }
  ],
  "message": "string"
}
```

| » code       | string                                        | false | none | <br /> | none  |
| » data       | \[[PublicVoucher](#schemapublicvoucher)]¦null | false | none | <br /> | none  |
| »» id        | integer                                       | true  | none | <br /> | none  |
| »» threshold | number                                        | true  | none | <br /> | 门槛    |
| »» value     | number                                        | true  | none | <br /> | none  |
| »» claimable | boolean                                       | true  | none | <br /> | 是否可领取 |
| »» validDays | integer                                       | true  | none | <br /> | none  |
| » message    | string¦null                                   | false | none | <br /> | none  |

# 管理积分系统（用户端）

## GET 获取我的积分账户信息

GET /api/points/account/my

查询当前登录用户的积分余额，返回当前用户的总积分、冻结积分等信息。后端需从 Token 解析 userId

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "userId": 0,
    "totalBalance": 0,
    "frozenBalance": 0
  },
  "message": "string"
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称               | 类型                                    | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明       |
| ---------------- | ------------------------------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | -------- |
| » success        | boolean                               | true  | none | <br /> | none     |
| » code           | string                                | true  | none | <br /> | none     |
| » data           | [PointsAccount](#schemapointsaccount) | true  | none | <br /> | 用户积分账户总览 |
| »» id            | integer(int64)                        | false | none | <br /> | none     |
| »» createTime    | string(date-time)                     | false | none | <br /> | none     |
| »» updateTime    | string(date-time)                     | false | none | <br /> | none     |
| »» creator       | integer(int64)                        | false | none | <br /> | 创建人      |
| »» updater       | integer(int64)                        | false | none | <br /> | 更新人      |
| »» userId        | integer(int64)                        | false | none | <br /> | 关联用户ID   |
| »» totalBalance  | integer(int64)                        | false | none | <br /> | 当前可用总积分  |
| »» frozenBalance | integer(int64)                        | false | none | <br /> | 冻结积分     |
| » message        | string¦null                           | true  | none | <br /> | none     |

## GET 分页查询积分明细

GET /api/points/record/my

分页展示积分获取和消费的记录

### 请求参数

| 名称   | 位置    | 类型      | 必选 | 说明                       |
| ---- | ----- | ------- | -- | ------------------------ |
| page | query | integer | 是  | 页码, default 1            |
| size | query | integer | 是  | 每页条数, default 20         |
| type | query | string  | 否  | 筛选类型：EARN/CONSUME/EXPIRE |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": [
    {
      "id": 0,
      "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "creator": 0,
      "updater": 0,
      "userId": 0,
      "type": "EARN",
      "amount": 0,
      "relatedId": "string",
      "description": "string"
    }
  ],
  "message": "string"
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称             | 类型                                     | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明           |
| -------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ------------ |
| » success      | boolean                                | true  | none | <br /> | none         |
| » code         | string                                 | true  | none | <br /> | none         |
| » data         | \[[PointsRecord](#schemapointsrecord)] | true  | none | <br /> | \[积分变动流水记录]  |
| »» id          | integer(int64)                         | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| »» createTime  | string(date-time)                      | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| »» updateTime  | string(date-time)                      | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| »» creator     | integer(int64)                         | false | none | <br /> | 创建人（通常为系统ID） |
| »» updater     | integer(int64)                         | false | none | <br /> | 更新人（通常为系统ID） |
| »» userId      | integer(int64)                         | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| »» type        | string                                 | false | none | <br /> | 变动类型         |
| »» amount      | integer                                | false | none | <br /> | 变动数量，正数或负数   |
| »» relatedId   | string                                 | false | none | <br /> | 关联业务ID（如订单号） |
| »» description | string                                 | false | none | <br /> | 文案描述         |
| » message      | string¦null                            | true  | none | <br /> | none         |

#### 枚举值

| 属性   | 值       |
| ---- | ------- |
| type | EARN    |
| type | CONSUME |
| type | EXPIRE  |
| type | REFUND  |

# 管理积分系统（管理员端）

## POST 新增积分规则

POST /api/points/admin/rules

创建新的积分发放/消耗规则

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "channelType": "ORDER",
  "ratio": 0,
  "expireDays": 0,
  "description": "string",
  "isEnabled": true
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称            | 位置   | 类型                | 必选 | 说明                   |
| ------------- | ---- | ----------------- | -- | -------------------- |
| body          | body | object            | 否  | none                 |
| » id          | body | integer(int64)    | 否  | none                 |
| » createTime  | body | string(date-time) | 否  | none                 |
| » updateTime  | body | string(date-time) | 否  | none                 |
| » creator     | body | integer(int64)    | 否  | 规则创建人 ID (管理员 ID)    |
| » updater     | body | integer(int64)    | 否  | 规则最后更新人 ID (管理员 ID)  |
| » channelType | body | string            | 否  | 触发渠道                 |
| » ratio       | body | number            | 否  | 兑换比例（如：1.0 表示 1元=1分） |
| » expireDays  | body | integer           | 否  | 有效期天数，-1表示永久有效       |
| » description | body | string            | 否  | 规则描述                 |
| » isEnabled   | body | boolean           | 否  | none                 |

#### 枚举值

| 属性            | 值        |
| ------------- | -------- |
| » channelType | ORDER    |
| » channelType | COMMENT  |
| » channelType | LOGIN    |
| » channelType | REGISTER |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "string",
  "data": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "channelType": "ORDER",
    "ratio": 0,
    "expireDays": 0,
    "description": "string",
    "isEnabled": true
  },
  "message": "string"
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称             | 类型                                   | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明                   |
| -------------- | ------------------------------------ | ----- | ---- | ------ | -------------------- |
| » success      | boolean                              | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| » code         | string                               | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| » data         | [PointsRule](#schemapointsrule)¦null | false | none | <br /> | 积分获取与消耗规则            |
| »» id          | integer(int64)                       | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| »» createTime  | string(date-time)                    | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| »» updateTime  | string(date-time)                    | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| »» creator     | integer(int64)                       | false | none | <br /> | 规则创建人 ID (管理员 ID)    |
| »» updater     | integer(int64)                       | false | none | <br /> | 规则最后更新人 ID (管理员 ID)  |
| »» channelType | string                               | false | none | <br /> | 触发渠道                 |

# 管理积分系统（系统内部）

## POST 订单完成（发放积分）

POST /api/inner/points/notify/order-success

订单系统调用此接口。积分系统内部会查找 channelType=ORDER 的规则，计算积分，创建 PointsRecord 和 PointsBatch

> Body 请求参数

```json
{
  "userId": 4,
  "bizId": "ORD_20231111_001",
  "amount": 99.5,
  "eventTime": "2023-11-11T10:00:00Z",
  "extraInfo": "{\"isDouble11\": true}"
}
```

### 请求参数

| 名称          | 位置   | 类型      | 必选 | 说明   |
| ----------- | ---- | ------- | -- | ---- |
| body        | body | object  | 否  | none |
| » userId    | body | integer | 是  | none |
| » bizId     | body | string  | 是  | none |
| » amount    | body | number  | 是  | none |
| » eventTime | body | string  | 是  | none |
| » extraInfo | body | string  | 是  | none |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "200",
  "message": "积分发放成功",
  "data": 99
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称        | 类型          | 必选   | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| --------- | ----------- | ---- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| » success | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » code    | string      | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » message | string¦null | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » data    | integer     | true | none | <br /> | none |

## POST 评价完成发放积分

POST /api/inner/points/notify/review-success

评价发布后调用，发放积分

> Body 请求参数

```json
"{\n  \"userId\": 1001,\n  \"bizId\": \"REV_556677\",\n  \"amount\": 0, // 评价可能不看金额，只看动作\n  \"eventTime\": \"2023-11-12T10:00:00Z\",\n  \"extraInfo\": \"{\\\"hasImage\\\": true, \\\"wordCount\\\": 50}\" // 规则引擎可能判断带图多给分\n}"
```

### 请求参数

| 名称          | 位置   | 类型      | 必选 | 说明            |
| ----------- | ---- | ------- | -- | ------------- |
| body        | body | object  | 否  | none          |
| » userId    | body | integer | 是  | none          |
| » bizId     | body | string  | 是  | none          |
| » amount    | body | integer | 是  | 评价可能不看金额，只看动作 |
| » eventTime | body | string  | 是  | none          |
| » extraInfo | body | string  | 是  | none          |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "200",
  "message": "评价积分发放成功",
  "data": 10
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称        | 类型          | 必选   | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明        |
| --------- | ----------- | ---- | ---- | ------ | --------- |
| » success | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none      |
| » code    | string      | true | none | <br /> | none      |
| » message | string¦null | true | none | <br /> | none      |
| » data    | integer     | true | none | <br /> | 表示增加了10积分 |

## POST 积分冻结（积分抵扣）

POST /api/inner/points/trade/freeze

用户在“确认订单”页面选择积分抵扣时调用。系统需按有效期优先原则（FIFO）锁定即将过期的积分

> Body 请求参数

```json
"{\n  \"userId\": 1001,\n  \"points\": 500,        // 用户希望抵扣500积分\n  \"tempOrderId\": \"TEMP_ORD_123456\" // 临时订单号/交易流水号\n}"
```

### 请求参数

| 名称            | 位置   | 类型      | 必选 | 说明          |
| ------------- | ---- | ------- | -- | ----------- |
| body          | body | object  | 否  | none        |
| » userId      | body | integer | 是  | none        |
| » points      | body | integer | 是  | 用户希望抵扣500积分 |
| » tempOrderId | body | string  | 是  | 临时订单号/交易流水号 |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "200",
  "data": {
    "success": true,
    "pointsUsed": 500,
    "moneySaved": 5,
    "balanceSnap": 2000,
    "message": "锁定成功"
  }
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称             | 类型          | 必选   | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明          |
| -------------- | ----------- | ---- | ---- | ------ | ----------- |
| » success      | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none        |
| » code         | string      | true | none | <br /> | none        |
| » message      | string¦null | true | none | <br /> | none        |
| » data         | object      | true | none | <br /> | none        |
| »» success     | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none        |
| »» pointsUsed  | integer     | true | none | <br /> | none        |
| »» moneySaved  | integer     | true | none | <br /> | 告知订单系统：减去5元 |
| »» balanceSnap | integer     | true | none | <br /> | 剩余可用        |
| »» message     | string      | true | none | <br /> | none        |

## POST 积分扣除

POST /api/inner/points/trade/deduct

支付成功后调用，将冻结状态转为实际扣除，并生成消费流水记录。

> Body 请求参数

```json
"{\n  \"userId\": 1001,\n  \"tempOrderId\": \"TEMP_ORD_123456\", // 对应之前的冻结记录\n  \"finalOrderId\": \"ORD_20231111_001\" // 最终生成的订单号（用于关联流水）\n}"
```

### 请求参数

| 名称             | 位置   | 类型      | 必选 | 说明               |
| -------------- | ---- | ------- | -- | ---------------- |
| body           | body | object  | 否  | none             |
| » userId       | body | integer | 是  | none             |
| » tempOrderId  | body | string  | 是  | 对应之前的冻结记录        |
| » finalOrderId | body | string  | 是  | 最终生成的订单号（用于关联流水） |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "200",
  "message": "积分扣除完成",
  "data": true
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称        | 类型          | 必选   | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| --------- | ----------- | ---- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| » success | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » code    | string      | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » message | string¦null | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » data    | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none |

## POST 积分解冻/回滚

POST /api/inner/points/trade/rollback

用户未支付/取消订单，或支付失败时调用。将冻结的积分释放回账户。

> Body 请求参数

```json
"{\n  \"userId\": 1001,\n  \"tempOrderId\": \"TEMP_ORD_123456\",\n  \"reason\": \"USER_CANCEL\" // 回滚原因\n}"
```

### 请求参数

| 名称            | 位置   | 类型      | 必选 | 说明   |
| ------------- | ---- | ------- | -- | ---- |
| body          | body | object  | 否  | none |
| » userId      | body | integer | 是  | none |
| » tempOrderId | body | string  | 是  | none |
| » reason      | body | string  | 是  | 回滚原因 |

> 返回示例

> 200 Response

```json
{
  "success": true,
  "code": "200",
  "message": "积分已回滚",
  "data": true
}
```

### 返回结果

| 状态码 | 状态码含义                                                   | 说明   | 数据模型   |
| --- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------ |
| 200 | [OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1) | none | Inline |

### 返回数据结构

状态码 **200**

| 名称        | 类型          | 必选   | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| --------- | ----------- | ---- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| » success | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » code    | string      | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » message | string¦null | true | none | <br /> | none |
| » data    | boolean     | true | none | <br /> | none |

```json
    },
    "remarks": "string"
```

<h2 id="tocS_Review">Review</h2>

<a id="schemareview"></a> <a id="schema_Review"></a> <a id="tocSreview"></a> <a id="tocsreview"></a>

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "customer": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
```

<h2 id="tocS_PointsRule">PointsRule</h2>

<a id="schemapointsrule"></a> <a id="schema_PointsRule"></a> <a id="tocSpointsrule"></a> <a id="tocspointsrule"></a>

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "channelType": "ORDER",
  "ratio": 0,
  "expireDays": 0,
  "description": "string",
  "isEnabled": true
}

```

积分获取与消耗规则

### 属性

| 名称          | 类型                | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明                   |
| ----------- | ----------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | -------------------- |
| id          | integer(int64)    | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| createTime  | string(date-time) | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| updateTime  | string(date-time) | false | none | <br /> | none                 |
| creator     | integer(int64)    | false | none | <br /> | 规则创建人 ID (管理员 ID)    |
| updater     | integer(int64)    | false | none | <br /> | 规则最后更新人 ID (管理员 ID)  |
| channelType | string            | false | none | <br /> | 触发渠道                 |
| ratio       | number            | false | none | <br /> | 兑换比例（如：1.0 表示 1元=1分） |
| expireDays  | integer           | false | none | <br /> | 有效期天数，-1表示永久有效       |
| description | string            | false | none | <br /> | 规则描述                 |
| isEnabled   | boolean           | false | none | <br /> | none                 |

#### 枚举值

| 属性          | 值        |
| ----------- | -------- |
| channelType | ORDER    |
| channelType | COMMENT  |
| channelType | LOGIN    |
| channelType | REGISTER |

<h2 id="tocS_PointsRecord">PointsRecord</h2>

```json
{
  "id": 0,

  "userId": 0,

  "description": "string"
}
```

| 名称          | 类型                | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明           |
| ----------- | ----------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ------------ |

| createTime  | string(date-time) | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| updateTime  | string(date-time) | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| creator     | integer(int64)    | false | none | <br /> | 创建人（通常为系统ID） |
| updater     | integer(int64)    | false | none | <br /> | 更新人（通常为系统ID） |
| userId      | integer(int64)    | false | none | <br /> | none         |
| type        | string            | false | none | <br /> | 变动类型         |
| amount      | integer           | false | none | <br /> | 变动数量，正数或负数   |
| relatedId   | string            | false | none | <br /> | 关联业务ID（如订单号） |
| description | string            | false | none | <br /> | 文案描述         |

#### 枚举值

| 属性   | 值       |
| ---- | ------- |
| type | EARN    |
| type | CONSUME |
| type | EXPIRE  |
| type | REFUND  |

<h2 id="tocS_PointsEarnDTO">PointsEarnDTO</h2>

<a id="schemapointsearndto"></a> <a id="schema_PointsEarnDTO"></a> <a id="tocSpointsearndto"></a> <a id="tocspointsearndto"></a>

```json
{
  "userId": 0,

  "amount": 0,
  "eventTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "extraInfo": "string"
}
```

### 属性

| 名称        | 类型                | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明                             |
| --------- | ----------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ------------------------------ |

| bizId     | string            | true  | none | <br /> | 业务ID（如订单号、评价ID），用于去重防止重复加分     |
| amount    | number            | true  | none | <br /> | 金额基数（如订单实付金额），用于计算积分：积分=金额\*比例 |
| eventTime | string(date-time) | false | none | <br /> | 事件发生时间，用于计算积分有效期               |

<h2 id="tocS_MerchantApplication">MerchantApplication</h2>

<a id="schemamerchantapplication"></a> <a id="schema_MerchantApplication"></a> <a id="tocSmerchantapplication"></a> <a id="tocsmerchantapplication"></a>

```json
{
  "id": 0,
  "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "creator": 0,
  "updater": 0,
  "deleted": true,
  "applicant": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  },
  "applicationExplain": "string",
  "applicationState": 0,
  "handler": {
    "id": 0,
    "createTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "updateTime": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
    "creator": 0,
    "updater": 0,
    "deleted": true,
    "username": "string",
    "authorities": [
      {
        "name": "string"
      }
    ]
  }
}

```

### 属性

| 名称                 | 类型                  | 必选    | 约束   | 中文名    | 说明   |
| ------------------ | ------------------- | ----- | ---- | ------ | ---- |
| id                 | integer(int64)      | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| createTime         | string(date-time)   | false | none | <br /> | none |
| updateTime         | string(date-time)   | false | none | <br /> | none |
| creator            | integer(int64)      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| updater            | integer(int64)      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| deleted            | boolean             | false | none | <br /> | none |
| applicant          | [User](#schemauser) | true  | none | <br /> | none |
| applicationExplain | string              | false | none | <br /> | none |
| applicationState   | integer(int32)      | false | none | <br /> | none |
| handler            | [User](#schemauser) | false | none | <br /> | none |
